2017年的WESG赛事以“世界竞在眼前”为口号，将包含《反恐精英：全球攻势》、《DOTA2》、《星际争霸II》和《炉石传说》4个竞技游戏项目，并新增《球球大作战》为首的移动游戏项目，其中《炉石传说》和《反恐精英：全球攻势》还将分为通用组和女子组，致力于打造与传统体育相同的竞技体系。"

In Asia Pacific Predator League 2018, the best DOTA 2 e-sports teams in Malaysia will be battling it out for a portion of the total prize pool of USD 150,000 . The winner of the Malaysian qualifiers will compete alongside other SEA teams from Indonesia, Thailand, India, Philippines , Hong Kong and Singapore."
